        <h3 class="s-post-summary--content-title">
         <a class="s-link" href="/questions/72193794/how-to-sort-arrays-of-objects-by-dates-but-with-most-current-date-first-in-javas">
          How to sort arrays of objects by dates but with most current date first in Javascript
         </a>
        </h3>
        <div class="s-post-summary--content-excerpt">
         I've got the array of objects:

       <div class="s-post-summary--content">
        <h3 class="s-post-summary--content-title">
         <a class="s-link" href="/questions/72193783/sorting-typescript-string">
          Sorting typescript string [][]
         </a>
        </h3>
        <div class="s-post-summary--content-excerpt">
         Const list = [[ ‘A1’ , ‘lorem’],[ ‘A11’ , ‘lopsum’],[ ‘A2’ , ‘dolum’]];
There is a way to sorting this array for getting this result:
[[ ‘A1’ , ‘dolum’],[ ‘A2’ , ‘lopsum’],[ ‘A11’ , ‘lorem’]]
        </div>
